  <meta content="The average parents tendency is to hide what goes on in their relationship from their children in the desperate hope that their children will do better than they have done. But it doesnt work like that! It never has. If you want to see your children have better relationships than you it is necessary to start by helping them learn more about the reality of love and relationship. You need to talk with them about how and why relationships work (and don\t work)." name="description"/>
